PHYI'I DE NYID BCU

GSUNGS PA NI, 'DIR GNYIS KA'I RGYUD CES GSUNGS PA RNAL 'BYOR

NYID BCU NI 'DRA BAR SNANG NGO, ,DE LA TING NGE 'DZIN NI DANG PO
SBYOR BA LA SOGS PA DANG, STANG STABS NI GA-YAS BRKYANG LA SOGS

MA'I SKU NI SEMS KYI CHA MI BRTAN PA DANG, RLUNG GI CHA GA-YO
BA BYED

PA'O ZHES RLUNG SEMS GNYES LA GSUNGS SO, ,KUN RDZOB DE'I BDEN
PA NI SKU DE CHU'I ZLA BA LTA BUR GSAL BAR SNANG ZHING MI SLU
BA'O, ,DON DAM PA'I BDEN PA NI, NANG STONG PA NYID NAS DNGOS
PO MED PA'I NGO BO NYID STONG PA NYID KYI BAR BCU DRUG DANG,
DE NAS

DNGOS PO STONG PA NYID DANG, DNGOS PO MED PA STONG PA NYID
GNYIS TE CHOS DANG GANG ZAG GNYIS KA'I BDAG GIS STONG PAS
STONG PA CHEN PO BCO BRGYAD DO, ,DON DAM PA DE'I MTHA' NI GNAS
SO, ZHES PA NI DON DAM BDEN PA STONG NYID DANG RO GCIG PA'I
DON GYI

@059A *, ,'OD GSAL GYI YE SHES ZUNG 'JUG GI RGYUR 'GYUR BAS
GNAS ZHES GSUNGS PA'AM, YANG NA DON DAM BDEN PA CHOS THAMS CAD
KYI RTZA BA DANG GZHI YIN PAS GNAS SO, ,DE LTAR RGYAN BDUN GYI
BSHAD THABS KYIS 'DUS PA'I RGYUD 'CHAD

PA'I TSUL YE SHES RDO RJE KUN LAS BTUS PA LA BRTEN NAS, SGRON
GSAL GYIS BSHAD PAR RGYUD NYUNG DU? 'DIR MED PA 'GA' ZHIG BKOD
PA NI RGYUD RGYAS PA NA YOD PAR MNGON LA, RGYUD KYI GZHUNG RE
RE LA MTHA' DRUG DANG, TSUL BZHI GANG RUNG GI BSHAD PA

SBYAR BA NI MGON PO KLU SGRUB KYI MAN NGAG LA YOD PA SGRON
GSAL DU BKOD PA YIN NO, ,GSUM PA LA GNYIS, ZHU BA, LAN NO,
,DANG PO NI, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' CHEN PO RNAMS KYIS GSOL PA,
DON DAM PA'I BDEN PA STE 'OD GSAL LA RAB TU GNAS

PA'I RNAL 'BYOR PA CHEN POS, LAS KYI RGYAL PO MCHOG GI TING
NGE 'DZIN LA BRTEN NAS, SEMS CAN GYI ZHI BA LA SOGS PA'I DON
JI LTAR SPYAD PAR BGYI ZHES ZHUS TE, 'DIS NI DON GYI 'OD GSAL
MNGON DU BYAS PA'I 'OG TU, DANG PO SBYOR BA

DANG DKYIL 'KHOR RGYAL MCHOG GIS GZHAN DON SGRUB PA GNYIS
KYANG 'PHEN PAS, RDZOGS RIM PA'I TING NGE 'DZIN GSUM KA STON
PAR GZUNG NGO, ,DES NA TING NGE 'DZIN GSUM GYI LHA'I RNAL
'BYOR LA BSKYED RIM DANG RDZOGS RIM GNYIS

SU YOD LA, DE YANG 'PHAGS PA YAB SRAS KYI GZHUNG NAS BSHAD PA
LTAR BSKYED RIM PAS SNGAGS KYI SKU DANG, RDZOGS RIM PAS YE
SHES KYI SKU SKYED PA'I LHA'I SKYED CHOG SO SOR SHES NA SHES
PA YIN TE, DE LTAR MI SHES PA RNAMS

@059B KYIS NI, LHA YI SKU SKYED PA'I CHO GA THAMS CAD BSKYED
RIM DU 'CHAD PAR SNANG NGO, ,GNYIS PA NI, BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS
LAN BKA' STZAL PA, JI SRID DU ZHI BA LA SOGS PA'I LAS KYIS
SEMS CAN GYI DON MI BYED PA DE SRID DU RNAL 'BYOR PA CHEN PO
DE YANG DAG PA'I

MTHA' 'OD GSAL LA MNYAM PAR BZHAG STE GNAS PAR 'GYUR RO, ,GANG
DU SEMS CAN GYI DON BYA BAR MTHONG NA DE'I TSE BDAG LA BYIN
GYIS BRLAB PA DAG PA'I SGYU MA'I SKU SKYED PA'I RIM GYIS YANG
DAG PA'I MTHA' 'OD GSAL LAS LANGS TE, ZHI RGYAS DBANG DRAG LA

SOGS PAS SEMS CAN GYI NAD ZHI BA DANG DPAL 'BYOR RGYAS PA SOGS
KYI DON BYAS NAS, YANG DAG PA'I MTHA' 'OD GSAL NYID DU 'JUG
PAR BYED DO, ,'DI MI SLOB PA'I ZUNG 'JUG LA SBYOR NA 'OD GSAL
LAS BZHENGS PA DANG, SLAR YANG 'JUG PA GZHAN

SNANG TZAM YIN TE, SANGS RGYAS RNAMS 'OD GSAL LA RTAG TU MNYAM
PAR BZHAG PA'I PHYIR RO, ,SLOB PA'I ZUNG 'JUG LA BYED NA SGRA
SOR BZHAG BYAS KYANG CHOG GO ,BZHI PA MJUG GI DON LA GNYIS,
RGYUD YONGS SU RDZOGS PA'I DON, GANG GIS BSGYUR BA'I

TSUL LO, ,DANG PO NI, RGYAN BDUN 'PHRES DANG BCAS PA GSUNGS
PA'I RJES DE NAS, BYAMS PA LA SOGS PA'I BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
CHEN PO RNAMS STON PAS LAN LAGS PAR BKA' STZAL PA DE LA DANG
POR DGA' ZHING BAR DU MGU LA THA MAR YI RANGS TE, ,

CHOS KYI DON NGES PA'I DBANG GIS SEMS LA DGA' BA DANG, YID BDE
BA SKYES NAS 'OD GSAL BA'I DON LA DMIGS TE CANG MI SMRA BAR
'KHOD PAR GYUR TO, ,DPAL YE SHES RDO RJE KUN LAS BTUS PA ZHES
BYA BA BLA NA MED PA'I RNAL 'BYOR CHEN

@060A *, ,PO'I RGYUD KYI RGYA CHER BSHAD PA LAS, BDE BA CHEN
PO STONG PA BZHI'I YE SHES DANG, SGYU MA'I SKU LA SOGS PA STON
PA'I LE'U STE RIM PA GNYIS PA'I RGYA CHER BSHAD PA'O, ,RDZOGS
SO ZHES PA NI YANG DAG

PAR GRUB PA'I DON NO, ,GNYIS PA NI, RGYA GAR GYI MKHAN PO
PAndI TA 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS KYIS BYIN GYIS BRLABS PA DZNY'A NA
KA RA'I ZHAL SNGA NAS DANG, ZHU CHEN GYI LO TZTSA BA KHU STON
DNGOS GRUB KYIS DANG POR RGYA SKAD LAS BOD SKAD DU BSGYUR
CING, TSIG

DON LA ZHUS DAG BYAS NAS, 'CHAD NYAN GYIS KYANG GTAN LA PHAB
PA, SLAD NAS BLA MA DE NYID DANG, LO TZ'A BA DGE SLONG NAG TSO
TSUL KHRIMS RGYAL BAS TSIG DON LA ZHUS DAG BYAS SHING 'CHAD
NYAN GYIS GTAN LA PHAB PA'O, ,YE SHES RDO RJE KUN LAS BTUS, ,

RNAL 'BYOR CHEN PO'I GSAL BYED YIN, ,YE SHES RANG BZHIN 'KHOR
BA DANG, ,MYA NGAN 'DAS PA'I NGO BO'O, ,DE GNYIS DBYER MED RDO
RJE STE, ,KUN 'DIR 'DUS PAS KUN LAS BTUS, ,DE STON PA LA DER
BTAGS NAS, ,GZHUNG LAS MING DON BA ? PA YIN, ,ZHES PA NI LO
TZ'A

BAS SBYAR BA STE, DON GO BAR SLA LA, RANG GI LUGS KYI MING DON
NI BSHAD ZIN TO,, ,,GANG ZHIG RTOGS NA RNAL 'BYOR CHEN PO'I
RGYUD, ,SHIN TU RTOGS DKA' RNAMS KYI 'CHAD TSUL LA, ,MA RMONGS
BLO GROS SNANG BA RGYAS 'GYUR BA, ,DE NI YE SHES RDO RJE KUN
LAS BTUS, ,

RGYUD DON KUN GSAL 'DAB STONG RAB RGYAS SHING, ,RIM GNYIS
SBRANG RTZI'I BCUD KYI ZIL MNGAR CAN, ,DRANG NGES 'BYED PA'I
DRI BSUNG RAB 'PHRO BA, ,RNAM BSHAD NYIN BYED 'OD KYIS LEGS
PAR PHYE, ,LUNG DANG RIGS PA'I 'DAB GNYIS BSKYOD PA YIS,
,GSUNG RAB DE NYID MKHA' LA LDING

@060B 'DOD CING, ZAB LAM SBRANG RTZI'I RO LA ROL 'DOD PA'I,
,SKAL BZANG BUD PA'I TSOGS RNAMS DGA' BAR GYIS, ,RTZA RGYUD
MTHAR THUG BSHAD TSUL MTHAR THUG GIS, ,BSHAD PA'I DGONGS PA
BDAG 'DRAS DPAG DKA' BAS, ,JI BZHIN MIN BSHAD 'GAL BA CI

MCHIS PA, ,DRI MED SPYAN LDAN KUN LA SNYING NAS BSHAGS, ,RDO
RJE 'CHANG DBANG 'PHAGS PA YAB SRAS LNGA'I, ,GZHUNG LA RING DU
'DRIS SHING KHYAD PAR DU, ,BSHAD RGYUD LNGA PO PHAN TSUN LEGS
BSGRIGS NAS, ,LEGS PAR BSHAD LAS ZLA ZER KUN TA LTAR,,

RAB DKAR DGE BA JI SNYED BSAGS PA DES, ,LAM GYI MTHAR THUG 'DI
DANG MI 'BRAL ZHING, ,SKAL BZANG RNAM DPYOD LDAN PA DU MA YIS,
,BSTAN PA'I SNYING PO YUN RING 'DZIN PAR SHOG ,CES DPAL YE
SHES RDO RJE KUN LAS BTUS PA'I RGYUD KYI RGYA CHER BSHAD

PA RGYUD BSHAD THABS KYI MAN NGAG GSAL BAR BSTAN PA ZHES BYA
BA 'DI NI, DPAL GSANG BA 'DUS PA'I RNAL 'BYOR PA SHAR TZONG
KHA PA BLO BZANG GRAGS PA'I DPAL GYIS, 'BROG RI BO CHE DGA'
LDAN RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I GLING DU SBYAR BA'I YI GE PA NI

DKA' BZHI PA RIN CHEN DPAL LO, ,'DIS KYANG BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE
PHYOGS DUS KUN TU RGYAS PAR BYED NUS PAR GYUR CIG , ,,SARBA
